DROP TABLE IF EXISTS zetetic_company;
CREATE TABLE zetetic_company
  (
     idx      INT NOT NULL auto_increment,
     name     VARCHAR(255),
     address  VARCHAR(255),
     country  VARCHAR(50),
     type     CHAR(1),
     category VARCHAR(6),
     employee INT,
     benefit  VARCHAR(30),
     asset    FLOAT,
     PRIMARY KEY (idx)
  ) engine=innodb charset=utf8mb4; 

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS zetetic_product;
CREATE TABLE zetetic_product 
  (
    idx         int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
    company_idx int NOT NULL ,
    code        varchar(6),
    PRIMARY KEY (idx),
    UNIQUE KEY uk_01 (company_idx, code)
  ) engine=innodb charset=utf8mb4; 

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS zetetic_announcement;
CREATE TABLE zetetic_announcement
  (
     idx          INT NOT NULL auto_increment,
     company_idx  INT NOT NULL,
     release_date DATE,
     content      TEXT,
     PRIMARY KEY (idx)
  ) engine=innodb charset=utf8mb4; 

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS zetetic_income;
CREATE TABLE zetetic_income
  (
     idx                INT NOT NULL auto_increment,
     company_idx        INT NOT NULL,
     report_date        DATE NOT NULL,
     revenue            FLOAT NOT NULL,
     cost_of_goods_sold FLOAT NOT NULL,
     gross_profit       FLOAT NOT NULL,
     operating_expenses FLOAT NOT NULL,
     operating_income   FLOAT NOT NULL,
     interest_expense   FLOAT NOT NULL,
     taxes              FLOAT NOT NULL,
     net_income         FLOAT NOT NULL,
     PRIMARY KEY (idx),
     INDEX list_01 (company_idx, report_date)
  ) engine=innodb charset=utf8mb4; 

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS zetetic_code;
CREATE TABLE zetetic_code 
  (
    idx   INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
    grp   VARCHAR(30),
    code1 VARCHAR(100),
    code2 VARCHAR(100),
    code3 VARCHAR(100),
    val   VARCHAR(10),
    PRIMARY KEY (idx),
    UNIQUE KEY (code1, code2, code3),
    INDEX list_01 (grp,code1,code2,code3)
  ) engine=innodb charset=utf8mb4; 

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS zetetic_work;
CREATE TABLE zetetic_work 
  (
    idx        int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
    publisher  varchar(20) NOT NULL,
    owner      varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
    task       varchar(100) NOT NULL,
    status     varchar(4) DEFAULT '0401',
    expected   varchar(10) NOT NULL,
    created timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
    updated timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT current_timestamp(),
    PRIMARY KEY (idx),
    INDEX list_01 (publisher),
    INDEX list_02 (owner)
  ) engine=innodb charset=utf8mb4; 

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS zetetic_campaign;
CREATE TABLE zetetic_campaign 
  (
    idx                  INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
    campaign_id          VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL      COMMENT 'origin campaign id',
    start_date           TIMESTAMP NOT NULL        COMMENT 'campaign start date',
    end_date             TIMESTAMP NOT NULL        COMMENT 'campaign start date',
    shop_name            VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL      COMMENT 'origin shop name',
    product_id           VARCHAR(30) NOT NULL      COMMENT 'origin product id',
    product_name         VARCHAR(300) NOT NULL     COMMENT 'origin product name',
    product_image        VARCHAR(300) NOT NULL     COMMENT 'origin product image url',
    price_org            VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL      COMMENT 'price of origin',
    price                FLOAT NOT NULL            COMMENT 'connector price',
    partner_cms_rate_org VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL      COMMENT 'partner commission rate of origin',
    partner_cms_rate     FLOAT NOT NULL            COMMENT 'partner commission rate',
    creator_cms_rate_org VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL      COMMENT 'creator commission rate of origin',
    creator_cms_rate     FLOAT NOT NULL            COMMENT 'creator commission rate',
    total_cms_rate       FLOAT NOT NULL            COMMENT 'partner commission rate + creator commission rate',

    created TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    updated TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),

    PRIMARY KEY (idx),
    UNIQUE KEY (campaign_id, product_id)
  ) engine=innodb charset=utf8mb4; 

DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS zetetic_procedure;
CREATE PROCEDURE zetetic_procedure( IN param_num INT, IN param_str VARCHAR(10) )
BEGIN
    DO SLEEP(5);
END;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS zetetic_mybatis;
CREATE TABLE zetetic_mybatis 
  (
    idx int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
    type varchar(2) NOT NULL COMMENT '01:select, 02:execute',
    l1 varchar(20) NOT NULL COMMENT 'level1',
    l2 varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'level2',
    l3 varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'level3',
    l4 varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'level4',
    obj text NOT NULL COMMENT 'json object',
    status int(1) DEFAULT 1 COMMENT '1:activated, 0:deleted',
    updated timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    PRIMARY KEY (idx),
    UNIQUE KEY l1 (l1,l2,l3,l4),
    KEY list_01 (status,type,l1,l2,l3,l4)
  ) engine=innodb charset=utf8mb4;

INSERT INTO zetetic_mybatis(type, l1, l2, l3, obj) VALUES ('01', 'product', 'list', 'time', 
'{"datetime":{"updated":"dd-MM-yyyy","start_date":"dd-MM-yyyy","end_date":"dd-MM-yyyy"},"value":{"market_id":{"type":"int"},"size":{"type":"int"},"offset":{"type":"int"}},"query":["SELECT up.id AS req_id, up.user_id, up.updated, up.status AS req_status, pd.* FROM ( SELECT id, user_id, promotion_id, status, updated FROM user_promotion WHERE user_id = #{@user_id} ORDER BY id ${order} LIMIT #{size} OFFSET #{offset} ) up LEFT JOIN ( SELECT p.*, m.currency AS currency, mc.descript AS type_descript FROM ( SELECT id, market_id, type, seq, title, image, start_date, end_date, CAST(cms_amount AS UNSIGNED) AS cms_amount, CAST(target AS UNSIGNED) AS target, descript, status FROM promotion WHERE market_id = #{market_id} ) p LEFT JOIN ( SELECT id, region, lang, currency FROM market ) m ON p.market_id = m.id LEFT JOIN ( SELECT key3 AS code, val1 AS descript FROM z_meta WHERE key1 = \'SRV\' AND key2 = \'PROD\' ) mc ON p.type = mc.code ) pd ON pd.id = up.promotion_id"]}' );
